I haven't had it long enough to know if that'll happen with mine; so a few months down the road I will update my review. A few tips: (1) to save wear and tear on the rope \\"handles\\", instead of hooking my hands inside the ropes, I just hold onto the ends of the \\"cloth\\" part of the scrubber--it's long enough to allow you to do that; (2) to prevent mold from growing on it, rinse the soap out before shutting off the shower, wring out the scrubber, and hang it to dry out--dries quickly this way--I just use rope handle on 1 end of scrubber to loop over a shampoo bottle top in my shower caddy, and the scrubber hangs free in the air and dries quickly. I don't like the soft material side, as it feels just like a wash cloth. As for the design I think its an interesting new take on most back scrubbers I've seen and is easy to store but they need to make more size variety with this, I feel, as they only have two different sizes (a 10x34 and a handheld mitt type).
